##### Biography

Idefons Cerda (1815–1876 CE) was a Spanish engineer, who wrote a paper in 1867 to describe the science of making cities. It is in this paper named 'General Theory of Urbanization' that he invented the word 'urbanization'. The term is used today to describe the process of expansion and redevelopment of cities. He issued only two volumes of the paper. The first was dedicated to urbanization as a fact, analysing how industrialization and new systems of mobility could transform cities.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//98824a4a-c47b-4f8a-bef0-109e2eabad2c/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_850_1207_1040_1400.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A28Z%2F-1%2F%2Fa2596ae05b662ec382f75204faf7e22127ba4fac80e8f19855557bc72dc2a828" alt="Image" width="15%" /></div>


#### Points to Remember

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//98824a4a-c47b-4f8a-bef0-109e2eabad2c/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_165_51_1187_1055.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A29Z%2F-1%2F%2F5010621d93fdf4aa1479a7efc78998ee92c2b0614304b01debb4e02b11ab3263" alt="Image" width="85%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//98824a4a-c47b-4f8a-bef0-109e2eabad2c/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_230_1094_297_1153.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A29Z%2F-1%2F%2Ff0a4cbac1d6c939527302b9d03416ac8da23afa9c2ef3ea0341c8dfbbac12d7f" alt="Image" width="5%" /></div>


##### Important Terms

Urbanization: The process in which more and more people start to live and work in towns and cities rather than villages

Rural: Connected with or like the countryside

Urban: Connected with a town or city

Primitive: Belonging to a very simple society with no Industry, etc.

Wetland: Relating to or existing in areas of land that are naturally wet

Satellite cities: Smaller cities that come around larger cities but are independent of them

Smart cities: Urban regions that are highly advanced in terms of overall infrastructure

# Natural and Man-made Disasters

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//1484e481-db05-47ba-9d38-78f19ca5fc07/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_131_295_219_391.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A27Z%2F-1%2F%2Fbce1ac4dffbc21669eeeaf6d6952d91c35cdaba4cf40a57c93b5a2f59ca3162d" alt="Image" width="7%" /></div>


##### Learning Outcomes

differentiates between natural and man-made disasters.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//1484e481-db05-47ba-9d38-78f19ca5fc07/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_385_535_454_603.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A27Z%2F-1%2F%2F1fa54da4d235e8a54b5f67f88ac45fb69cba84b1373f50a7e201e3169050e9dd" alt="Image" width="5%" /></div>


##### Recall

##### Skill: Communication

Talk about any disaster that may have occurred recently—floods or earthquakes or fire. What was the impact of this disaster on people and their belongings?

##### WHAT ARE DISASTERS?

Disasters are unexpected events that cause significant physical damage or destruction to life and property, or result in a drastic change in the environment. While most disasters, such as earthquakes, volcanic eruption, wildfires, and hurricanes happen suddenly, others, like droughts may have a slow beginning and later increase in extent and intensity.

Disasters have a long-term impact on the society, environment and economy of the affected region.

Disasters can have geological, geographical or man-made causes. Disasters can be broadly categorized into two types—natural and man-made. While floods, cyclones, earthquakes and droughts are natural disasters that happen with no human intervention, the man-made ones include train accidents, plane crashes, industrial or nuclear accidents, biological disasters, terrorist attacks and use of weapons of mass destruction.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//1484e481-db05-47ba-9d38-78f19ca5fc07/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_670_642_737_713.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A28Z%2F-1%2F%2F770a5acac6cb98590a099b33b1db239fc5d023a067d36d2281e32df0a3e9ac37" alt="Image" width="5%" /></div>


##### Quick Facts

Hybrid disasters result from both human error and natural forces. For example, the extensive clearing of forests causes soil erosion, which then causes landslide if there is a heavy rainfall.

Certain regions are prone to various hazards that may cause a disaster. Towns on the banks of rivers are prone to floods; places near the coast are prone to cyclones and tsunamis; places in the Himalayas are prone to earthquakes, landslides and avalanches; and places near volcanoes are always vulnerable to volcanic eruptions.

India is a highly disaster-prone country. About 65 per cent of the land area is vulnerable to earthquakes, 12 per cent of floods, 8 per cent of cyclones and 70 per cent of drought. Disasters affect people living underdeveloped countries more adversely than those in developed countries, mostly because underdeveloped countries do not have proper disaster management systems in place. It is, therefore, very important that people are made aware of the hazards and trained to take preventive measures in case of a disaster.

There are several effects of disaster:

t. loss of life;

2. injury to human beings and animals;

3. damage to property and infrastructure such, as dams, bridges, roads, railways, power and communication network,

4. environmental damage.

5. loss of livelihood and work,

6. psychological damage,

7. the outbreak of disease.

Let us take a look at the various kinds of disasters.

### NATURAL DISASTERS

<div style="text-align: center;"><div style="text-align: center;">Differences Between Natural and Man-made Disasters</div> </div>




<table border=1 style='margin: auto; word-wrap: break-word;'><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'></td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Natural Disasters</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Man-made Disasters</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Caused by</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Natural factors</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Human error/carelessness</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Scale of loss</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Large scale/huge devastation</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>less/localized destruction</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Duration</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Short or long</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Usually short, but can be of large magnitude</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Signals</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Occurs suddenly</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Sometimes provides signals</td></tr></table>

Natural disasters are events caused by natural forces that have major effects on the human population, infrastructure and biodiversity in an area. Earthquakes, floods, cyclones and droughts are some of the major natural disasters.

##### Types of Disasters



<table border=1 style='margin: auto; word-wrap: break-word;'><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Natural</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Man-made</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Earthquakes

##### Earthquakes

An earthquake is a sudden, violent movement of a portion of the earth's crust caused by a disturbance under the earth's surface. At times earthquakes take a heavy toll on life and property. Besides causing extensive damage to houses, large buildings, bridges, dams, rail lines and power lines, as well as communication networks, earthquakes can also act as hazards by triggering landslides, avalanches, and tsunamis.

The study of earthquakes is called seismology. Seismologists use seismographs to record earthquake shocks. The scale on which the intensity of the earthquake is measured is called the Richter Scale. The point on the earth's surface where the effects of an earthquake are felt most strongly is called the epicentre. Maximum damage on the surface of the earth occurs near the epicentre. A strong earthquake with a 7.1 magnitude struck Mexico on 20 September 2017, that killed more than 200 people and caused extensive damage to the buildings. Mexico is prone to earthquakes with magnitudes as high as 8.1 on the Richter Scale.

##### Causes of earthquakes

The surface of the earth is made up of interlocking plates of rock that float on a semi-liquid layer called the mantle. When two floating plates collide, the vibrations pass through the earth's surface or the crust. This makes the crust, along with everything on it, shake uncontrollably. Poorly constructed structures are usually the first to collapse during an earthquake.

##### Earthquake zones in India

The entire Himalayan belt is on the boundary between the Eurasian and the Indian plates

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//1484e481-db05-47ba-9d38-78f19ca5fc07/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_168_325_1152_1541.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A29Z%2F-1%2F%2Fd47cac1fc580f34b95a07b1416cbf605b54603121794a8ad38ffc4fab179f520" alt="Image" width="82%" /></div>


Earthquakes and Seismic zones in India

and is, therefore, prone to earthquakes. It falls under the very-high risk zone (Seismic Zone V). Because of frequent seismic activity, the region is also prone to avalanches and landslides, which cause severe damage to life and settlements in the area. Kachchh in Gujarat and the Ganga-Brahmaputra basin are in the high-risk zone (Seismic Zone IV). The map on the previous page shows the different earthquake zones of India. Strong earthquakes have caused great loss of life and property in the country. Buildings have collapsed and roads, bridges, communication and railway lines have been badly damaged. In some cases, dams have also burst. In the past few years, major earthquakes have occurred in Bhuj (2001), Uri (2005), Andaman Islands (2006), Sikkim (2011), Nepal (2015) and Assam (2021), causing tremendous loss of life and property.

##### Floods

A flood occurs when a sudden influx of water submerges land, posing a danger to life and property. When floodwater submerges towns, villages and farms, it forces people to move to other areas. It also washes away the top layer of the soil, which is the most fertile. When the residents finally return after the floodwater has receded, they discover that their belongings have been damaged, and the crops ruined. Many people also lose their lives if they are not able to move to a safe place in time.

Floods are mostly caused due to the overflowing of rivers in the monsoon. These are called riverine floods. They are caused due to heavy rains in the monsoon. With the onset of the south-west monsoons many parts of India receive heavy rainfall, leading to floods in many rivers. People living in low-lying areas in the river basins suffer the most. The loss of life and property is huge. At times, the fertile top soil is removed by the fast-flowing waters, leaving the land infertile. The south-west monsoon causes most of the floods in the flood plains of the rivers Brahmaputra, Ganga, Yamuna, Mahanadi and the rivers of Punjab. Heavy rains created a flood-like situation in India's financial capital, Mumbai, in the monsoon season of 2017, causing massive disruption to normal life. It forced authorities to shut down schools and colleges as heavily-used suburban trains—the city's lifeline—came to a halt. More than 14 people lost their lives in these floods, which also wrecked homes and caused total chaos in the city.

Apart from monsoon rains, floods are also caused when there is a breach in a dam, when there are very high tides near the coast due to cyclones, when there is a change in the course of a river due to landslides, earthquakes or when there is sudden melting of huge masses of snow. Flash floods are sudden floods resulting from any of these factors and cause heavy damages.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//a30afe0c-9018-4cd4-814a-327d91608d18/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_545_955_638_1032.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A27Z%2F-1%2F%2F67a2152b735860ec0355e1883eb0aa77e018603380cfb6a1bd976768ce278792" alt="Image" width="7%" /></div>


#### Did You Know?

In August 2018, Kerala experienced the worst floods in a century due to intense monsoon rains and the release of waters from dams. Over 5 million people were affected and about 440 people died. In August 2020, Assam experienced severe floods due to heavy rains and rising water levels of the Brahmaputra River. Over 5.5 million people were affected and more than 100 people died. These floods killed many wild animals at the Kaziranga National Park and large parts got submerged.

##### Cyclones

Cyclones are low-pressure areas that occur over warm ocean waters of temperate and tropical regions. Seen as swirling atmospheric

disturbances that are oval or circular in shape, they are accompanied by heavy rain, huge waves, and powerful winds blowing at a velocity of 300 km per hour. Storm surges during the high tide, called storm tides, causes enormous damage to coastal regions.

India has a coastline of about 7,516.6 km. This long coastline is prone to very severe cyclonic formations in the Bay of Bengal and the Arabian Sea. West Bengal, Odisha, Andhra Pradesh and Tamil Nadu are the states in India most vulnerable to cyclones.

##### Droughts

Droughts are caused when a region receives insufficient rainfall for a long period of time. Shortage of water in drought-prone areas leads to a fall in the water table, crop failure, and therefore, a shortage of food, fodder, employment. As people begin to starve, the migrate to other places and become homeless. People in villages who are completed dependent on agriculture and animals husbandry and tribals who are dependent. Forests for resources are worst affected due to drought.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//a30afe0c-9018-4cd4-814a-327d91608d18/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_194_519_1066_1628.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A27Z%2F-1%2F%2F6076933a71a7f9d971542a00b1a8fc2717ef17078e8d24a6d6dbe7b97536a723" alt="Image" width="73%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><div style="text-align: center;">Regions in India showing other natural disasters</div> </div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//a30afe0c-9018-4cd4-814a-327d91608d18/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_0_58_507_349.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A28Z%2F-1%2F%2F8bf312b541b53837d9becb240ebb006b02c02e530d37f58dafce06d4cbfe137d" alt="Image" width="42%" /></div>


Droughts happen due to a prolonged period of rainfall shortage.

Droughts are caused not only by shortage of rainfall but also due to deforestation, misuse of groundwater, unscientific agricultural practices, etc.

The states worst affected by water scarcity in India are Rajasthan, Gujarat, Chhattisgarh, Madhya Pradesh, Maharashtra, Karnataka, and Odisha. About 30 per cent of the land area in India is drought-prone. Floods and droughts occur almost every year, bringing with them epidemics and causing human suffering.

In 2022, European countries like Italy, France, Portugal experienced the worst drought in centuries. Rivers Po, Rhine and Danube had very low water levels.

##### MAN-MADE DISASTERS

Crises caused by human acts—intentionally or unintentionally, are called man-made disasters. The leakage of a hazardous gas from a chemical factory or a fire in a restaurant can be classified under the unintentional man-made disaster category. On the other hand, the effects of a planned nuclear explosion can be termed as an intentional man-made disaster. All kinds of man-made disaster leads to a tremendous human suffering and huge loss of life and property. Disasters also have an adverse impact on the economy of the nation.

##### Fires

The most common kind of disaster, fires, can break out anywhere—at homes, offices, hospitals, or recreational centres. Casualties in such incidents rise if the place is crowded, and there are few exit points. One such incident was the Uphaar cinema hall tragedy in New Delhi on 13 July 1997. Fires usually occur due to poor wiring and faulty electrical equipment, leakage of cooking gas or a carelessly thrown matchstick. The most common cause of a fire in a building is poor electrical wiring and faulty equipment. Electrical wiring must be regularly checked. If the wiring is wornout, it must be replaced immediately by standard quality wires and electrical fittings to avoid any short-circuit.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//a30afe0c-9018-4cd4-814a-327d91608d18/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_547_674_1067_1013.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A28Z%2F-1%2F%2Fe6fd44aa40cbe66d289a007c46e166fdb9a639d6729e57b0283551bf5d76b5d5" alt="Image" width="43%" /></div>


Poor electrical wiring is a major cause of fire.

Fire is also caused due to gas leakage. Gas pipes, regulators and stoves should be regularly checked to ensure no leakage. Regular maintenance checks in gas pipelines should also be mandatory. Fire is also commonly caused by carelessly thrown matches and cigarettes. It is also one of the common causes of forest fires.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//a30afe0c-9018-4cd4-814a-327d91608d18/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_558_1362_653_1432.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A28Z%2F-1%2F%2F7bcd2d1592e3bb72d8753e562cd22841aa78b74aea62de8d2d2f796b21fbb4e7" alt="Image" width="7%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//a30afe0c-9018-4cd4-814a-327d91608d18/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_799_1345_872_1412.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A28Z%2F-1%2F%2Ffe7b797fde727e3389719ea17e203a0bee4002df05d29a621bc50a67f0631e11" alt="Image" width="6%" /></div>


What are the ways by which you can save yourself and your family when a gas leak happens at home?

There are also fire-related disasters in areas where wood is used in construction activities. The loss of life is more if a fire breaks out in crowded areas.

##### Nuclear Disasters

A disaster caused by the use of nuclear weapons is called a nuclear disaster. Nuclear weapons are weapons of mass destruction (WMD) and lead to mass destruction of life and property. The adverse effects of nuclear radiation through the use of these weapons leave thousands of people crippled for life. Several thousands suffer throughout life due to exposure to radiation. A nuclear explosion is so bright that it can make people blind if they see it with the naked eye. The explosion is followed by a heat wave and a huge cloud formation at the blast site. In such a disaster, radioactivity is the silent killer whose effects continue for a very long time after the incident. The energy released in the form of particles from the radioactive elements such as uranium, plutonium, etc. is called radioactivity. It spreads in the area and causes nausea, dizziness, vomiting and disorientation. It is very harmful to human health and causes serious illnesses like cancer.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//a30afe0c-9018-4cd4-814a-327d91608d18/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_95_1058_614_1447.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A28Z%2F-1%2F%2Fb58e41d15dce85e812fc0cc54571d3bc01dfb8a3d76da0aa65d6b95a8b65e8a5" alt="Image" width="43%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><div style="text-align: center;">A nuclear bomb explosion</div> </div>


The worst type of man-made disaster, it can cause the collapse of social, political and economic establishments across the globe. Crises of this kind could occur intentionally as well as unintentionally.

A prime example of an intentional nuclear disaster is the attack on Hiroshima and Nagasaki in Japan by the United States during World War II. Around one lakh people died, and an equal number were injured when fighter planes dropped two bombs-nicknamed 'Little Boy' and 'Fat Man'—on the two Japanese cities. Unintentional nuclear disasters mostly occur due to accidents in nuclear power reactors. In 1986, an accidental explosion at a nuclear plant in Chernobyl in the former USSR caused radiation to spread across Ukraine and other regions. As many as 12,000 Ukrainians died in the Chernobyl disaster. In the event of a nuclear disaster, one should close all the doors and windows of their houses and remain indoors as radiators do not penetrate solid structures. People should not go out until the government makes arrangements for their rescue.

##### Chemical and Biological Disasters

Disasters caused by the accidental release of toxic chemicals or gases into the environment from factories or other establishments are known as chemical disasters. Some industries produce hazardous substances that cause harm to human beings as well as the environment. If these substances accidentally released into the environment they travel fast and cause large-scale devastation.

The Bhopal gas tragedy (1984), which was caused by the accidental leakage of a highly toxic gas called methyl isocyanate from the Union Carbide factory in the capital of Madhya Pradesh, left about 2,500 people dead. The effects of a chemical disaster could extend to several future generations.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//a30afe0c-9018-4cd4-814a-327d91608d18/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_11_79_523_474.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A29Z%2F-1%2F%2F5a69b1f5165f6d19c547cd9e714a9b68c6df8ba1122f26b9e046ce864b6d4763" alt="Image" width="43%" /></div>


Old victims of the Bhopal gas tragedy during a rally to mark the 26th year of the Bhopal Gas Disaster, in Bhopal in 2010

Biological disasters are caused by germs developed in laboratories and released into the air to kill a large number of people. When these microbes are inhaled by a person or get absorbed in his/her system through a cut or wound, they can infect him/her. Even a few drops of the smallpox or plague virus could start an epidemic, killing thousands of people.

##### Oil Spill

Oil spills occur when large quantities of oil are discharged into oceans or seas during drilling operations, cleaning of tankers and leaks from pipelines and storage tanks. An accident or explosion on a tanker or an offshore drilling rig can also result in massive oil spills.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//a30afe0c-9018-4cd4-814a-327d91608d18/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_24_1132_100_1219.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A29Z%2F-1%2F%2F1e812b79ce50de538030649ebc62d5cda87e5b7166e296c88c2589c11355be4d" alt="Image" width="6%" /></div>


##### Knowledge of India

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//a30afe0c-9018-4cd4-814a-327d91608d18/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_389_1129_531_1210.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A29Z%2F-1%2F%2F31e99a05312d0e835612a6fbaab8c532c5f8688bd425620fe164c7c6ff75eeee" alt="Image" width="11%" /></div>


Suraj Prakash Vaid, a 66-year-old taxi driver in Delhi, is known as 'the man of the golden hour'. His dedication to helping people during emergencies, especially in the crucial first hour after an accident, has earned him this nickname. He carries a first-aid kit and travels on a scooter to beat traffic. He has saved many people till date. He is a compassionate individual and urges people to call him in case of an accident or trauma.

as happened in the case of the Deepwater Horizon in 2010. Most cases of oil spills are severe cases of man-made disasters as they cause long-term damage to the ocean and its marine life. Some of the chemicals from the oil kill many forms of marine life and coral reefs. Other chemicals leave a residual black layer on the feathers of birds and the fur of mammals, causing them to die or drown. If an oil spill reaches the coast, it destroys fishing and tourism. Unfortunately for the earth, oil spills have happened quite frequently, with a few major spills having taken place off the coasts of the US. However, the Deepwater Horizon case is now considered to be one of the worst spills to have happened in recent times.

##### Terror Attacks

This kind of disaster occurs in the event of a terror strike, either through the use of explosives, guns, or chemical and biological weapons. Most of these disasters are brought about by misdirected elements who think that social, political, or religious goals can be achieved by killing people. Terrorists also hijack planes and destroy public infrastructure, such as railway tracks and bridges, to cause massive devastation.

The attack on the World Trade Centre in the US on 11 September 2001, when terrorists hijacked planes to spread terror, resulted in nearly 3,000 deaths. The most destructive terror attacks in India include the attack on Parliament on 13 December 2001, and the Mumbai attacks on 26 November 2008.

##### Travel-related Disasters

Some examples of travel-related disasters are air crashes, train collisions and derailments, capsizing of boats and ships, etc. All these travel-related disasters adversely impact a large number of people. Accidents during

train, road, and flight journeys are very common. When such an accident results in the death of a large number of people, it becomes a disaster. Most of these incidents occur due to equipment failure, loss of radar transmission in planes, or failure of brakes in buses, human error (driver falling asleep while driving or missing a railway signal), fuel leakage, or natural phenomena (earthquakes, storms, or landslides).

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//5ded67ed-a6b1-454d-8c29-9a6d4260a115/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_98_430_645_775.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A26Z%2F-1%2F%2Ff3131ccf2d36757e7ba38b2fb6ad4907591acaedfac354829b1e962b95130245" alt="Image" width="45%" /></div>


Excavators working to remove rail compartments after the Balasore train accident in June 2023.

## CASE STUDIES OF NATURAL AND MANMADE DISASTERS

#### The Nepal Earthquake

The Nepal earthquake was a devastating earthquake that struck near Kathmandu, the capital of Nepal, on 25 April 2015.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//5ded67ed-a6b1-454d-8c29-9a6d4260a115/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_102_1146_647_1539.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A26Z%2F-1%2F%2F900e171be9f9b581a2d59ac9f675b986f712df58ebd643537b2b1de3776dd4b3" alt="Image" width="45%" /></div>


A map showing the epicentre of the earthquake in Nepal, in 2015

Nearly 9,000 people were killed and several thousands more were injured. The earthquake destroyed over 600,000 small and large buildings, and other structures in Kathmandu and nearby areas.

1. The initial shock registered a magnitude of 7.8. The epicentre of the quake was about 77 km northwest of Kathmandu, and the focus was about 15 km underground.

2. Two large aftershocks, with magnitudes 6.6 and 6.7, were felt in the region within an hour of the main quake.

3. Several smaller aftershocks were experienced in the region during the succeeding days.

4. The collision of the earth's plates caused the earthquake in Nepal. The Indian plate is moving northward under the Eurasian plate at a speed of 4.5 cm per year.

5. Nepal lies on the fault called 'Thrust Fault', where a sudden release of energy along the fault resulted in one plate jumping over the other. The earthquake devastated Nepal and tremors were felt across India, Bangladesh, south-west China and Pakistan.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//5ded67ed-a6b1-454d-8c29-9a6d4260a115/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_673_1011_1190_1523.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A26Z%2F-1%2F%2F0a8410b46055a6f6b2e7401b74b9e708f9879136e119c5c4481e3a4f1bd5a8f9" alt="Image" width="43%" /></div>


△ The Nepal earthquake caused a lot of damage to life and infrastructure.

##### Think and Answer

Himachal Pradesh experienced devastating floods in 2023. What according to you was the reason: nature or human intervention?

#### The Deepwater Horizon disaster

The offshore Macondo oil rig called Deepwater Horizon in the Gulf of Mexico exploded after a blowout and tragically killed 11 workers, besides injuring 16 more. Also known as the BP oil spill since the rig was owned by BP P.L.C. or British Petroleum, this is considered the largest oil spill in the history of the petroleum industry. An estimated 4.9 million barrels of oil was discharged into the water. The spill started in April 2010 and could only be contained and the oil rig was scaled in September 2010. The spill resulted in severe environmental, health and economic consequences. There was extensive damage to marine wildlife, and fishing and tourism industries were adversely affected.

The long-term effects of this disaster could still be felt in 2013.

1. It has been reported that about 4.6 million pounds of oily material was removed from nearby beaches in Louisiana.

2. Oil was even found on beaches far off from the Macondo site. Even in 2013, dolphins and other marine life continued to die in record numbers.

3. BP P.L. C. or British Petroleum was found guilty of cost-cutting and inadequate safety system, and legal proceedings are still continuing.

#### Floods in Assam and Bihar

Devastating floods cause massive damages to the states of Assam and Bihar every year.

##### Flood in Assam

Heavy rainfall in Assam causes the Brahmaputra River and its tributaries to overflow. The Brahmaputra River is the lifeline of Assam. As the river enters Assam, it becomes braided, at 6-km wide, and along with its tributaries, creates a flood plain 80-100 km broad and almost 1,000 km long.

The 2020 Assam floods were devastating for the people and environment in the region.

1. The floods affected over 5 million people, displacing nearly 2 lakh. Some 150 people lost their lives in the flood.

2. The floods also caused extensive damage to infrastructure, crops, and livestock.

3. The heavy rains also caused landslides in several areas of the state. These landslides blocked roads and bridges, making it difficult to provide relief in the affected areas.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//5ded67ed-a6b1-454d-8c29-9a6d4260a115/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_591_772_1121_1210.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A27Z%2F-1%2F%2Fc68a6bf0bb270633de565aaf6112ac881d512e9ee7f25f0d4ee8ac61faf7535b" alt="Image" width="44%" /></div>


The Assam floods were devastating for the people and the environment.

4. The floods also caused several health problems, as people were forced to use contaminated water. Children's education was affected as many schools were closed due to the floods, and many children had to miss school for weeks.

##### Flood in Bihar

Bihar is the most flood-prone state in the great northern plains of India. Almost 73 per cent of Bihar's total geographical area is affected by floods.

There are several reasons for this.

1. Bihar is affected by floods more than the other north Indian states because many of the rivers flowing through Bihar, such as the Kosi, Bagmati and Gandak, flow through the high, mountainous region of Nepal, before crossing very small distances and rapidly reaching the plains of Bihar, making them far more forceful.

2. When it rains very heavily in Nepal, the extra water enters these river channels and rushes into the plains of Bihar.

3. As the rivers break their banks and overflow into the adjoining areas, large swathes of land and thousands of people and livestock are affected.

4. More than 76 per cent of the population in northern Bihar live under the threat of floods every year and 68,800 sq km out of a total of 94,163 sq km of geographical area in Bihar is flooded every year.

In the most recent flood, more than 60 people died and more than 29,000,000 people were affected. Several districts, including Purnea, Kishanganj, Araria, Madhepura, Darbhanga, Madhubani, Supaul, Bhagalpur and Muzzafarpur were affected by the floods. The floods inundated more than 130 villages and led to the displacement of more than 52,000 people, who had to take shelter on higher ground.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//5ded67ed-a6b1-454d-8c29-9a6d4260a115/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_663_569_739_636.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A28Z%2F-1%2F%2F47ede13373b68b3aa5713531a876d26445b398066a314ea8c18ea901b945ffdc" alt="Image" width="6%" /></div>


##### HOTS Question

Skill: Critical Thinking

How can we stop the occurrence of disasters resulting from human activities such as deforestation and urbanization?

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//5ded67ed-a6b1-454d-8c29-9a6d4260a115/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_95_845_206_962.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A28Z%2F-1%2F%2F7d6c532daf4c1ba572ebc656d73e4a687254ea0e479f2bdd251416c10f22a5b3" alt="Image" width="9%" /></div>


#### Values and Life Skills

Development and disasters seem to go hand in hand. We need clean nuclear power and we also need pesticides to grow crops, but there is always the chance of a Chernobyl or a Bhopal gas tragedy happening.

What is the solution? Can we make a difference to the world by thinking differently about what is really important, and what is not?

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//5ded67ed-a6b1-454d-8c29-9a6d4260a115/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_117_1196_207_1281.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A28Z%2F-1%2F%2Fb0adf7a479369587d9f92115aedcf2074fce573a5f730c6bca8e1ec5861b006b" alt="Image" width="7%" /></div>


#### Biography

John Milne (1850–1913 CE) was a British geologist, mining engineer and seismologist. He is known as one of the most significant contributors to the study of earthquakes and developed the first international network for seismological data. He is known to have created the world's first modern seismograph in 1880, a machine with a simple horizontal pendulum that recorded vibrations which occur with sudden movements along the fault line in the earth.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//5ded67ed-a6b1-454d-8c29-9a6d4260a115/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_1000_1246_1188_1490.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A28Z%2F-1%2F%2F356d723cfd0fda1a1b1ddd02581f8b0620305f18935792408c0fc15194c7a07c" alt="Image" width="15%" /></div>


## Points to Remember

Disasters are unexpected events that cause significant physical damage or destruction to life and property, or result in a drastic change in the environment.

Disasters are due to geology, geographical conditions and man-made causes.

There are different types of disasters: Natural and man-made

Natural disasters are events caused by natural forces that have major effects on the human population, infrastructure and biodiversity in an area.

Earthquakes are sudden, violent movements of a portion of the earth's crust, caused by a disturbance under the earth's surface.

Floods occur when a sudden influx of water submerges land, posing a danger to life and property.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//5ded67ed-a6b1-454d-8c29-9a6d4260a115/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_107_85_1086_1186.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A28Z%2F-1%2F%2F98724fd10887c2d52881098c0b578d594b3af2d368fe724987df0adf25861ee2" alt="Image" width="82%" /></div>


Cyclones are low-pressure areas that occur over warm ocean waters of temperate and tropical regions.

Droughts are caused when a region receives insufficient rainfall for a long period of time.

The most common kind of disaster, fires, can break out anywhere.

Man-made disasters are those disasters caused by a human act, intentionally or unintentionally.

A disaster caused by the use of nuclear weapons is called a nuclear disaster. Nuclear weapons are weapons of mass destruction.

Disasters caused by the accidental release of toxic chemicals or gases into the environment from factories or other establishments are known as chemical disasters.

This kind of disaster occurs in the event of a terror strike, either through the use of explosives, guns, or chemical and biological weapons.

Some examples of travel-related disasters are air crashes, train collisions and derailments, capsizing of boats and ships, etc.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//5ded67ed-a6b1-454d-8c29-9a6d4260a115/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_118_1192_172_1264.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A28Z%2F-1%2F%2F4411c84abc071b54d82b370d778c2decf4a45189de2ebe698aeab67e918486ac" alt="Image" width="4%" /></div>


#### Important Terms

Avalanche: A fall or slide of a large mass, as of snow or rock, down a mountainside

Tsunami: A long, high sea wave caused by an undersea earthquake or other disturbance

Storm surge: An abnormal rise in the level of the sea along a coast caused by the onshore winds of a severe cyclone

Water table: The level below which the ground is saturated with water

Epidemic: An outbreak of a contagious disease that spreads rapidly and widely

Hazardous: Dangerous

#### EXERCISES

##### SAMS KENNISING ART U.S. © 1995

## A. Choose the correct option.

Choose the correct option.

1. Droughts are caused by insufficient ___ over a long period of time.

(i) flood (ii) storm (iii) rainfall (iv) sunlight

2. In 1986, an accidental explosion at a nuclear plant at ___ in the former I. caused radiation to spread across Ukraine and other regions, killing over 12,000 people.

(i) Kiev (ii) Chernobyl (iii) Astana (iv) St Petersburg

3. Chemical disasters are caused by ___

(i) gases (ii) germs (iii) pollen (iv) virus

4. Biological disasters occur when ___, which are grown in laboratories, get released in the air.

(i) chemicals (ii) germs (iii) pollen (iv) blossoms

5. Chemicals from ___ kill marine life and coral reefs and also affect birds and mammals.

(i) cyclones (ii) drought (iii) earthquakes (iv) oil spills

## B. Identify who I am.

1. I shake the ground, causing quite a fright. With a sudden jolt, any day or night. You will find me coming from the earth's crust. Guess who I am, causing the seismic thrust.

2. I swirl and spin, a powerful display. With ferocious winds, I come your way. Over the oceans and seas, I start my spree. Guess who I am, a weather mystery.

## C. Fill in the blanks.

1. Some disasters like ___ may begin slowly and later increase in extent and intensity.

2. Earthquake is an example of a major ___ disaster.

3. Cyclones are ___ areas that occur over warm ocean waters of temperate and tropical regions.

4. The ___ of the earth's plates caused the earthquake in Nepal in April 2015

5. The ___ gas tragedy was caused by the accidental leakage of a highly toxic gas called methyl isocyanate from the Union Carbide factory.

### D. State whether the following are true or false. Rewrite the false statements correctly.

1. Earthquakes also trigger landslides, avalanches, and tsunamis.

2. Floods wash away the top layer of the soil, which is the most infertile.

3. West Bengal is most vulnerable to floods.

4. Oil spills harm marine life.

5. The attacks carried out on Hiroshima and Nagasaki by the United States during World War II were an example of unintentional nuclear disaster.

# THEME 5: NATURAL AND MAN-MADE DISASTERS

6

# Disaster Management

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//f2d40ca2-86e1-4ea3-8333-1ab76dafbb27/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_21_295_72_400.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A30Z%2F-1%2F%2Fe19c0aef16cf57b0166eee0a5da5451eca77a7e543dea44bbadaab9647613e6d" alt="Image" width="4%" /></div>


### Learning Outcomes

#### The learner:

discusses the importance of disaster management.

lists measures to be taken to prevent disasters.

onstrates (through drills) measures to be taken in case of an earthquake, flood or fire.

explains the role of the government in disasters and its management.

### Recall

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//f2d40ca2-86e1-4ea3-8333-1ab76dafbb27/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_220_529_291_603.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A31Z%2F-1%2F%2F503355fec81e419b24028bf5bb7c2d019cf57eda7a70b2d5f59a691c209bf723" alt="Image" width="5%" /></div>


##### Skill: Compensation

Vaya's school was conducting an earthquake preparedness drill. They were showing students how to duck beneath tables, use corners and not create panic on the stairs. Do you think Maya's school is doing the doct thing?

Disaster management is the overall preparedness to handle the possibility of a disaster and efficient management of affected regions, as well as people, if such an incident were to occur. It involves plans and steps taken before, during and after a disaster to reduce the extent of suffering and damage. In the event of a disaster, the people, the government and social organizations need to work together to contain its impact.

## IMPORTANCE OF DISASTER MANAGEMENT

A disaster—whether natural or man-made—can strike anytime without warning. The geographical location and landscape of India exposes it to earthquakes as well as many kinds of weather-related disasters. When a natural disaster occurs in a developing country like India, it is usually the poor who suffer the most. Therefore, it is extremely important

for the government, the people and social organizations to be prepared with proper plans and arrangements to face any kind of disaster. Proper and prior planning can help in limiting and minimizing damages and losses resulting from any disaster—natural or man-made.

##### SAFETY MEASURES

When disasters strike, it usually takes everyone—the government, the people and different relief organizations—some time to respond. However, much of the impact of a disaster can be mitigated if everyone remains alert and generally prepared to cope with the different kinds of disasters that can occur. Hence, it is important to be adept in first-aid techniques, as well as the different safety measures that people can adopt in the event of a disaster.

The government undertakes various mitigation steps to counter the different types of disasters. A special department for disaster management is set up to tackle the disaster-related incidents. Funds are set aside for providing relief and disaster management. There are advanced warning and sound forecasting systems in place in disaster-

prone areas. There are many organizations which provide relief and rehabilitation work in case of these terrifying events. The government also creates public awareness about disaster preparedness through its various programmes. There are disasters that are region-specific. The community also must be well prepared to deal with disasters. People here should be equipped with medicines, food, shelter material, etc. Non-governmental organizations (NGOs), the Red Cross Society, UN agencies, the police and the Army have always assisted in such situations.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//f2d40ca2-86e1-4ea3-8333-1ab76dafbb27/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_125_563_225_656.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A31Z%2F-1%2F%2F48ef456ae583b9dc187fa456cd0698541e78ba47b89337e0cd53795a45f0efb9" alt="Image" width="8%" /></div>


##### Knowledge of India

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//f2d40ca2-86e1-4ea3-8333-1ab76dafbb27/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_525_556_668_642.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A31Z%2F-1%2F%2F97d56fb9479f0448d39966375a72cc2bf8c0b685488e5f3d8bd52af5336deeaf" alt="Image" width="12%" /></div>


The Government of India enacted the Disaster Management Act in 2005, which led to the creation of the National Disaster Management Authority (NDMA) and State Disaster Management Authorities. The primary purpose of NDMA is to coordinate efforts to control and mitigate the destruction caused by natural or man-made disasters. It is also the highest body in the country to make policies, plans and guidelines for disaster management to ensure timely and effective response to disasters in India.

#### Safety Measures During Earthquakes

If you are indoors during an earthquake, three steps—drop, cover and hold—could save you from receiving severe injuries. If your building is shaking, immediately drop to the ground and take cover under a bed or table. If you are outdoors during a tremor, the best strategy would be to move towards an open area—away from trees, buildings, transmission towers, electricity poles, etc. Stay away from bridges and flyovers during an earthquake and even after it has subsided.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//f2d40ca2-86e1-4ea3-8333-1ab76dafbb27/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_702_35_1190_335.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A32Z%2F-1%2F%2F660ee7bb72fb3a0ad7e4bfdeab5b486bd68eacfd0d09afe3e42ed1c61d5b3b75" alt="Image" width="41%" /></div>


▲ Drop, cover and hold technique for earthquark

It is very important to follow proper normal while constructing buildings, bridge flyovers and dams. Old buildings should be strengthened through the process retrofitting. We must keep a first-aid box home and in school. It can be very useful case of an emergency.

Even a mild earthquake can cause injuries people and damage buildings. Therefore, is necessary to take certain steps that can useful and help in minimizing the loss.

1. We can move out to an open place quickly as possible and also help others do the same.

2. In case of any injuries, we should administer first aid to the injured once we all are out the open.

3. We can return to our building after some time, if we feel that there is no danger after shocks.

4. We should check our building for damage and if we feel it is unsafe, we should move out immediately.

5. We should not go near snapped wires if we smell gas leaks, we should switch all stoves, lights and electrical gadgets.

6. One should always stay calm, call for help and offer aid to people in relief camps.

#### Safety Measures to Prevent Floods

The sudden influx of water during a floc poses considerable danger to life and proper

It is essential to prevent toடை contain the losses resulting from it.

Floods can be prevented in vulnerable areas by properly maintaining dykes and embankments along rivers.

The government and relief organizations must also have provisions for flood shelters in vulnerable places (along flood-prone regions), so that people and livestock can be quickly evacuated and provided relief to.

The government must also station rescue equipment near flood-prone areas. It should be possible to immediately deploy rescue boats and have communication lines open and functioning in order to rescue people caught in rising levels of water.

There should be enough dry food, clean water and medicines made available to the people, affected by floods, so that spread of diseases can be stopped.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//f2d40ca2-86e1-4ea3-8333-1ab76dafbb27/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_16_817_515_1094.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A32Z%2F-1%2F%2F7e4bf265b3881814b46818ff0701b2d064ddd744bbd69c6453e309af4a7b89ca" alt="Image" width="41%" /></div>


Delhi faced severe flooding in mid-2023.

They should be familiar with the terrain in order to quickly reach safer places in case of a flood.

People living in flood-prone areas should be prepared to handle floods.

A long stick should be kept handy to wade safely through floodwaters.

All electrical mains must be switched off to avoid short-circuits.

One should keep track of all the warnings about the flood given through TV and radio.

People can save household items and valuables by placing them at a height.

Toilets should be blocked with sandbags to prevent any backflow of sewage.

One should be careful of snakes, as snake-bite is common during floods.

- Sufficient essential supplies of food, water and medicines should be stored in case there is a threat of flood in an area.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//f2d40ca2-86e1-4ea3-8333-1ab76dafbb27/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_530_435_627_513.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A33Z%2F-1%2F%2F436151127197bd06d43529753e81a4a9d880aaa0eaf4bc546bd2e124eef1fe24" alt="Image" width="8%" /></div>


##### Did You Know?

Himachal Pradesh was devastated by floods in July 2023. Over 100 deaths were reported in the state. The estimated loss of the damage in the state was reportedly over 3,700 crore. The government initiated rescue and relief operations, with 20 NDRF teams, two ITBP teams and many helicopters for the same.

#### Safety Measures to Prevent Droughts

Unlike most of the other natural disasters, a drought is not a sudden occurrence. It takes a longer time for drought to set in and affect people. Therefore, it is possible to prepare in advance to mitigate the impact of a drought.

Using water sources such as rivers, lakes and ponds carefully and maintaining them is important to tide people over during times of no rain.

• Rainwater harvesting goes a long way in replenishing the depleting supply of groundwater. The government and social welfare organizations should teach and enable people to harvest rainwater to restore their water reserves.

Building of check dams also helps to collect run-off water in hilly areas.

- We should stop cutting down trees along river banks and other water bodies. Instead, we should plant more trees. Trees help in drawing moisture and rainfall to a region.

- We should stop wasteful use of water in our daily life.

##### Safety Measures During Cyclones

In order to mitigate the impact of cyclones, the following precautions can be taken:

People living in cyclone-prone regions must be alert and keep a track of warnings, announcements and instructions from the meteorological department and the Disaster Warning System (DWS), television news and radio broadcasts. They should carefully follow the instructions given on radio and television and act accordingly to avoid danger. A timely warning can save many lives.

- Cyclone-prone areas should have preconstructed shelters that are known to everyone.

The houses in these areas should be designed to withstand strong winds. If the houses are built as per safety norms, people can stay inside their homes, otherwise they should shift to shelters.

We must conserve coastal vegetation such as mangrove forests as these act as windbreaks and reduce the impact of waves.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fe73565c-7554-41f3-996e-d04fa10c6561/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_132_1049_201_1117.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A26Z%2F-1%2F%2Ffc3b99e6c052f3b3b07a5f2d6666ef5544b104fb853ca928030b637d072c261a" alt="Image" width="5%" /></div>


##### Quick Facts

#### Safety Measures to Prevent a Fire

In 2023, tropical Cyclone Biparjoy hit Gujarat and the surrounding areas, unleashing powerful gusts of wind that uprooted trees and electricity poles. The heavy rain accompanying the cyclone turned many roads into rivers and people were seen wading through waist-deep water. However, the timely preparation of government agencies and security forces saved the state from large-scale damage.

- Emergency kits, food, water and medicines should be kept ready in a waterproof bag.

People should take precautions against snakebites, fallen electric poles, wires, etc. A fire-related disaster is one of the most common amongst man-made disasters. However, a few precautions and steps go a long way in both preventing and/or minimizing damages occurring from a fire.

• Everyone should be acquainted with the common fire safety norms.

We should take some time out to find out about the different kinds of fire extinguishers and the correct ones to use in case of a fire. Fires are of different origins, and we should make an effort to know more about this and the right extinguisher to use.

A fire extinguisher

While entering a public place such as a cinema hall or auditorium, we should make note of the fire exits and all other possible exits.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fe73565c-7554-41f3-996e-d04fa10c6561/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_1038_360_1190_710.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A26Z%2F-1%2F%2F46f9044e31a2a8dd5af79ca77fc7065290ee2f36ff07a81627a97e61ce36add7" alt="Image" width="12%" /></div>


- If a fire were to break out, we should avoid using the lift as a means of escape.

We should undergo training in first-aid in case of a fire and ways to put out flames.

If we light a matchstick to light a candle or the stove, we should also make sure that the matchstick is properly disposed of.

We should always turn off the knob of our LPG cylinders when it is not in use. We should also always keep a kitchen window open so that any inflammable gas can dissipate instead of accumulating in the kitchen.

People should be trained in extinguishing fires of different origins or categories, such as an electrical fire, a fire caused by gas leaks, oil leaks, etc.

- One should never throw water on a fire caused by an electrical short-circuit.

If a person's clothes catch fire, he/she should be rolled over on the ground to extinguish the fire.

If the building catches fire, it must be evacuated immediately through the staircase. Lifts should never be used in case of fire.

If we see any outbreak of fire in our neighbourhood, we should immediately call the fire tender and inform the police.

We must always immediately inform the proper authority of any gas leakage, snapped electrical wires, etc., in our locality.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fe73565c-7554-41f3-996e-d04fa10c6561/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_8_601_63_680.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A27Z%2F-1%2F%2F001fdd93f64f714e0ce1169c44f3902af7f7698ad1af28cce95cd8009f924e2f" alt="Image" width="4%" /></div>


#### Think and Answer

Do you think India is well prepared to handle disasters? Give reasons for your answer.

Skills: Discussion and Debate

### Safety Measures in Case of a Nuclear Disaster

In case of a nuclear disaster, we can take the following precautions:

It is advisable to stay indoors with all doors and windows shut as radioactivity cannot penetrate through solid walls.

Any dust or liquid that gets deposited outside should not be touched as it may be contaminated.

Official broadcasts for instructions should be followed.

Nuclear plants should not be established in populated areas and such plants should never be constructed in an earthquake-prone region.

## Safety Measures in Case of a Chemical Disaster

In case of a chemical disaster, we can take the following precautions:

Chemical industries should not be allowed to function in populated areas.

The government should be equipped and must have a proper plan to handle emergencies. It should be prepared with antidotes and other relief measures in case of poisoning.

The government agencies should conduct regular safety and pollution checks of these chemical industries.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fe73565c-7554-41f3-996e-d04fa10c6561/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_496_443_591_528.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A27Z%2F-1%2F%2F779c6b72ff5edcca340024ee6f699da9bd673f47eec804ed442919e1740fd7cd" alt="Image" width="7%" /></div>


Natural disasters cannot be prevented, but measures can be taken to eliminate or reduce the possibility of trouble. In case of an emergency or disaster, what should be the most common preventive measures in your opinion? What type of evacuation plan and drill should be in place?

### Safety Measures in Case of a Biological Disaster

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fe73565c-7554-41f3-996e-d04fa10c6561/markdown_1/imgs/img_in_image_box_926_498_1002_574.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A27Z%2F-1%2F%2Fe2098364172679003d788be85f103e76399a4e77f4ce5d2258dcb46a3822c2e4" alt="Image" width="6%" /></div>


In case of a biological disaster, we can take the following safety measures:

People should inform the police and get away from any suspicious material that they see around them.

The government should educate people through the mass media in case of a threat of a biological attack.

People should not inhale such organisms and protect themselves by covering their faces.

### Safety Measures in Case of Terror Attacks

In case of a terror attack, we can take the following precautions:

People should always be alert and report to the concerned authorities about any suspicious persons in their neighbourhood.

- Any unattended bags or articles should not be touched and should immediately be reported to the police.

- All important telephone numbers such as those of police, ambulance, neighbours, etc. should be kept handy.

### Safety Measures in Case of Travel-related Disasters

In case of a travel-related disaster, we can take the following precautions:

- Victims should be safely evacuated from the site of the accident and first aid should be administered at the earliest.

- We should always carry our identity cards with the blood group mentioned on it. Emergency contact numbers should be written on the identity card to get in touch with family or friends.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fe73565c-7554-41f3-996e-d04fa10c6561/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_107_769_206_842.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A28Z%2F-1%2F%2Fb245799a073cb983b54a7e11354cc05af35be310cede0182e23077c4edd236bf" alt="Image" width="8%" /></div>


##### Did You Know?

A School Disaster Management system is the process of assessing and planning, physical protection and response capacity development designed to: 1. protect students and the staff from physical harm; 2. minimize disruption and ensure the continuity of education for all children; 3. develop and maintain a culture of safety

##### ROLE OF THE GOVERNMENT

The government must be fully prepared to tackle various kinds of disasters at all times. Governments of developing countries should allot a substantial sum of money from their budgets to set up special disaster management departments. Funds should also be set aside for relief and disaster management. Efficient forecasting and warning systems should be installed and modern tools of information technology must be used for managing such situations.

Besides this, the government should set up organizations to coordinate relief work and give top priority to rehabilitation and reconstruction plans. The communication network should be strengthened to ensure that entire regions do not get cut off in the eventuality of disasters like earthquakes and tsunamis.

Here are some ways in which a government can prevent man-made disasters:

Send inspection teams regularly to public establishments such as hotels, theatres, and hospitals to check if they adhere to safety regulations.

- Ensure that such establishments have all the required safety equipment, such as fire exits, extinguishers, and sand buckets, in place to fight a disaster.

- Make arrangements to ensure that no region under its jurisdiction suffers from a lack of fire stations or personnel.

- Check plans of buildings—especially multistoreyed ones—thoroughly for defects that may lead to a collapse. The government also needs to ensure that substandard building material is not used during construction.

Not all disaster-mitigation measures require government intervention; a lot can be achieved if people themselves take the initiative.

##### ROLE OF THE PEOPLE

At most times when a disaster occurs, the first people to cope with it are the victims themselves—often without the benefit of external aid. Hence, each of us should be adept in first-aid techniques and in ways to help other critically injured people.

1. Every house should have an emergency first-aid kit.

2. Some members of society should be familiar with basic first-aid procedures.

Besides this, awareness can also go a long way in mitigating disasters. For example, the management of a hotel could help save a lot of lives in the eventuality of a fire if it abides by government regulations on emergency exits, escape routes and fire extinguishers.

3. The residents of a war zone may construct underground bunkers that can protect them from air strikes by enemy nations.

4. People living in areas prone to tsunamis may plant more trees, or create tsunami walls, along the coastline to prevent extensive damage.

Most importantly, in today's context, it would be greatly helpful if people are alert to suspicious elements, such as terrorists, who are capable of launching attacks and causing man-made disasters.

### ROLE OF SOCIAL ORGANIZATIONS

There are various groups such as the Red Cross, UN agencies, and non-governmental organizations (NGOs) which provide aid at the time of disasters. These organizations focus on meeting people's emergency needs. They provide shelter, food, and medicines to the victims. They work to decrease the sense of isolation and abandonment that disaster victims often feel.

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//fe73565c-7554-41f3-996e-d04fa10c6561/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_535_458_604_531.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A28Z%2F-1%2F%2F75e76680af4fb3873e6a42a55155c067876419a8b7fcec8211f34865893920c4" alt="Image" width="5%" /></div>

#### Disaster Management at a Glance



<table border=1 style='margin: auto; word-wrap: break-word;'><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Safety Measures</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Prevention</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Role of Government and Social Agencies</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Have an emergency kit ready with food, water, first-aid supplies, torch, blanket and other essentials.</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Identify potential hazards in your area and take steps to mitigate them. Retrofit buildings and re-locate people away from the hazard area.</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Develop and implement disaster management plans at the district, state and national levels. Local governments should also prepare village-level disaster management plans.</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Know the location of emergency exits and have a plan for where to go in case of an emergency.</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Educate the public on preparedness and response, through training programmes or public awareness campaigns.</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Coordinating relief efforts with other government agencies, NGOs and International agencies</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Create safe shelter areas and inform everyone where to gather or go to in the event of a potential hazard.</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Conduct mock drills and exercises such as evacuations due to fires, earthquakes etc.</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Provide financial assistance to affected communities; coordinating distribution of food and essential supplies, providing psychological and social support to affected industries.</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Stay informed about the developments in the news and emergency alerts.</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Implementing building codes, land-use regulation and environmental conservation measures.</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Establishing and maintaining emergency communication systems.</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Ensure access to emergency supplies and equipment.</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Encourage insurance and risk management practices.</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Conducting post-disaster assessments and analytics.</td></tr></table>

#### Values and Life Skills

Certain basic necessities can keep you safe in a disaster. If you have these, you can save your own, and others' lives too. You also need courage and preparedness.

How can you help the other members of your family, including your pets, in the event of an earthquake?

George William Manby (1765–1854 CE) was an English author and inventor. In 1813, he invented the 'Extincteur', the first pressurised fire extinguisher or the first modern form of a fire extinguisher. It consisted of a copper vessel with 3 gallons of pearl ash (potassium carbonate) solution contained with compressed air. Manby's invention significantly improved the ability to fight fires and save lives.

##### Important Terms

Mitigation: A reduction in unpleasant or serious incident, event, etc.

Retrofitting: Reinforcing old buildings with new parts and equipment to strengthen them and make them safe

Aftershocks: A small earthquake that happens after a bigger one in the same area

Dyke: A long wall or embankment built to prevent flooding from the sea

 $ R^{2} $ water harvesting: The process of collecting and storing rainwater for future use

Windbreak: A row of trees, a fence, etc., that provides protection from the wind

Antidote: A substance that controls the effects of poison or disease

# THEME 6: ASIA—THE LARGEST CONTINENT

Asia—Location, Extent

Political and Physical Features

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//7603d27a-37ac-422f-82ab-2068ad64e0c8/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_122_294_210_387.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A29Z%2F-1%2F%2F0a74a615020ee44f48564316dc0d6d4d94d744df33553f02bf4fc30ec66217f2" alt="Image" width="7%" /></div>


##### Learning Outcomes

##### The learner:

identifies countries of Asia on the globe and on the world map.

"locates physical features, e.g. important mountains, plateaus, deserts, rivers, lakes, islands, on the map of Asia.

##### Recall

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//7603d27a-37ac-422f-82ab-2068ad64e0c8/markdown_3/imgs/img_in_image_box_376_552_445_620.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A29Z%2F-1%2F%2F4575f562df509dc9218b8355a9ab2c77255f051f2a55cf732df3c5497c0569ff" alt="Image" width="5%" /></div>


##### skill Communication

Look at the map of Asia in your atlas and answer the following:

1. Which country has the largest area in Asia?

2. Which country in Asia has the least population?

Asia is the largest continent in the world. It occupies about one third of the total land area of the world. It stretches between latitudes  $ 10^{\circ} $S– $ 80^{\circ} $N and longitudes  $ 25^{\circ} $E– $ 170^{\circ} $W, and has an area of approximately 45.03 million sq. km. The continent also has the largest population—an estimated 4.7 billion (mid-2021), which is roughly about 60 per cent of the world's total population. An outstanding feature of the geography of Asia is the great variety and diversity in physical, cultural,

and economic characteristics. This indeed makes it a 'continent of contrasts'.

##### LOCATION

Ural Mountains and the Caspian Sea in the west, and the Caucasus Mountains in the south-west. The Arctic Ocean lies to the north of Asia, while the Pacific Ocean and the Indian Ocean lie to the east and south of Asia, respectively.

Asia lies almost wholly in the northern and eastern hemispheres. Together with Europe, it is often referred to as Eurasia. It is separated from Europe by the

Latitudinally, Asia extends from  $ 10^{\circ} $S to  $ 80^{\circ} $N. Its east-west extent is 9,700 km. It extends from  $ 25^{\circ} $E to about  $ 170^{\circ} $W. There is a time difference of about 11 hours between the Anatolian Plateau (Asia Minor) in the west and the Pacific Coast in the east.

There are 48 independent countries in Asia. They vary in size from Russia, China, and India, which are the largest; to Singapore, the Maldives and Bahrain, which are the smallest. Some countries such as Japan, the Philippines.

Indonesia consists of a group of islands or archipelago. Most of the Asian countries were independent of the Indian peninsula was partitioned and after the Indian peninsula was divided into the USSR and the other regions into the other诸国. In 1991, the USSR broke up into several independent republics, some of which were in Europe and some in Asia.

### REGIONAL DIVISIONS

The countries of the largest continent are often grouped into East Asian countries, North Asian countries, Central Asian countries, South-East Asian countries, South

Asian countries and countries of West Asia.

The countries of Asia can, therefore, be divided into different groups based on their locations.

#### East Asia

The eastern part of Asia, consisting of several countries like China, North and South Korea, Japan and Mongolia makes up East Asia. This region also has the most varied vegetation in the world, even though rapid deforestation has destroyed much of the forests. East Asia has some of the world's busiest cities, such as Tokyo, Beijing, Shanghai and Hong Kong and has a population of about 1.6 billion people.

#### North Asia

North Asia comprises the Asian part of Russia, which includes Siberia and the Russian Far East. North Asia is divided by a long mountain range known as the Ural Mountains, lying in a north-south direction. The western part of Russia lies in the west of the Ural Mountains while the larger part, consisting of Siberia, lies in the east. Its location in the sub-Arctic region makes the winters long and severe, with heavy snowfall, while the summers are short and cool. The extreme winter conditions make this region sparsely populated, with a population of only about 38 million people.

#### Central Asia

Central Asia consists of several landlocked countries. These are Kazakhstan, Uzbekistan, Kyrgyzstan, Tajikistan, Turkmenistan and Afghanistan. The region extends from the Caspian Sea to the border of western China. More than 60 per cent of Central Asia comprises deserts, while the remaining 40 per cent is grasslands. It has the Altai Mountains.

in the east, which mainly lies in Kyrgyzstan and Tajikistan. The two main rivers of Central Asia are the Amu Darya and the Syr Darya. The rivers are very important to the Central Asian countries as the region remains quite dry for most of the year. Central Asia has a population of about 67.3 million people.

The countries of South-East Asia fall into two different sections. The northern part, which is a part of mainland Asia, consists of Vietnam, Laos, Cambodia, Thailand and Myanmar (previously known as Burma). The southern

##### South-East Asia

part consists of the island countries, Malaysia, Singapore, Brunei, Indonesia, Timor and the Philippines. South-East is bound by the Indian Ocean on the and the Pacific Ocean in the east. This has an abundance of tropical rainforests a wide variety of wildlife. The population this region is about 1,823 million.

#### South Asia

South Asia refers to the southern Asia countries of India, Pakistan, Nepal, Sri Lanka, Bhutan, Maldives and Bangladesh. This is home to about one-fifth of the world's

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//46c64e33-ba77-4478-b468-389e40bc7691/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_167_593_1178_1530.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-10T19%3A13%3A28Z%2F-1%2F%2F4628e5aa380092f94b1d4d01bdaf1c0b5e61c4b3af9bacf87de26eb3ce184fbb" alt="Image" width="84%" /></div>


<div style="text-align: center;"><div style="text-align: center;">Asia: Political</div> </div>


population, which is around 1.8 billion people and is the most densely populated region in the world. It is bounded on the north by the Timmalayan Mountains, to the east by the Bay of Bengal, to the west by the Arabian Sea and to the south by the Indian Ocean. South Asia also has a wide variety of natural vegetation and wildlife.

### West Asia

West Asia, also called Western Asia, comprises Armenia, UAE (United Arab Emirates), Yenten, Azerbaijan, Bahrain, Lebanon, Oman, Cyprus, Syria, Turkiye, Georgia, Iran, Israel, Jordan, Kuwait, Qatar and Saudi Arabia. This region has a population of about 257.23 million people. This region is not densely populated because of its inhospitable climate.

#### Quick Facts

The concentration of salt in the Dead Sea is so high that you will not drown in it; you will remain afloat because of natural buoyancy. It is called the Dead Sea because fish and aquatic plants cannot survive in it.
